		birth = yes

	}

		}
	}

	210.3.14 = {
		death = {
			death_reason = death_old_age
		}
	}
}

westernimperial_aversarinas_aagiokrata_3 = { # Old supporter of Aeschraes and a hardcore Magi in his own right. He was already considered ancient by the time the ICW started and the shock of Frod put him into a coma. His death causes his rather widespread holdings in Etepezea and Kalathipsomi to collapse, especially as no strong claimants remain to his name. Dragged his dynasty up from relatively obscure and disgraced counts in the early 12th century to owning half of northern Etepezea, especially capitalizing on Aeschraes nuking everyone he didnt like. Will probably be p dope in earlier bookmarks
	name = "Bathonex"
	religion = "aversarinas_aagiokrata"
	culture = "westernimperial"

	1099.10.21 = {
		birth = yes
		trait = intellect_good_3
		trait = beauty_good_1
		trait = magic_good_11
		trait = albino
	}

	1117.10.21 = {
		trait = gh_historical_school
		effect = {
			set_variable = { name = historical_magic_school value = flag:living_magic }
			set_variable = { name = historical_magic_school_min_spells value = 10 }
		}
		trait = education_stewardship_4
		trait = gh_historical_track_beasthunter_3
		trait = ambitious
		trait = diligent
		trait = zealous
		trait = flagellant
		trait = gh_historical_pilgrim_1
		trait = gh_historical_blademaster_3
	}

	1192.3.16 = {
		trait = gh_ritual_scars_1
		trait = gh_ritual_tattoos
		trait = scarred
		give_nickname = nick_firedrake
		effect = {
	  		add_character_flag = {
				flag = had_nickname_event
	  		}
		}
	}

	1200.1.1 = {
		trait = incapable # Frodbrokna broke him mentally, throwing him into a coma
	}

	1201.3.4 = {
		death = {
			death_reason = death_incapable
		}
	}
}
